add_namespace = sprd #dometstic
add_namespace = sprf #foreign
add_namespace = sprc #civil war

#Events affecting other countries are under 'Foreign Policy'

# Introduction event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.1
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.1"
	}
	title = sprd.1.t
	desc = sprd.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_alfonso_xiii

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.1.a
	}
	option = { #flavor
		name = sprd.1.b
		SPR = { country_event = { id = sprd.1163 days = 1 }}
	}
}

# Black Monday hits Spain
country_event = {
	id = sprd.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.2" }
	title = sprd.2.t
	desc = sprd.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.2.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_ideas = SPR_black_monday
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1181
				days = 3
			}
			set_country_flag = SPR_flag_black_monday_is_here
		}
		complete_national_focus = SPR_Crossroads_of_Chaos
	}
}

# Nerd Council Event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.3" }
	title = sprd.3.t
	desc = sprd.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 14
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR_nerd_council_setup = yes
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.3
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # mil focus
		name = sprd.3.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year }
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
		
		set_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3a_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_equipment_upgrade_xp_cost = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_war_support_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_army_factor = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # navy focus
		name = sprd.3.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year }
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
		
		set_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3b_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_equipment_upgrade_xp_cost = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_navy_org_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_navy_factor = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # air focus
		name = sprd.3.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year }
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
		
		set_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3c_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_air_range_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_air_factor = 0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_air_superiority_efficiency = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # nuclear focus
		name = sprd.3.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year }
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
		
		set_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3d_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_nuclear_production_factor = 0.15 }
		}
	}
	option = { # general focus
		name = sprd.3.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year }
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
		clr_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
		
		set_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3e_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_speed_factor = 0.025 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.15 }
		}
	}
	option = { # continue current focus
		name = sprd.3.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_mil_focus_this_year
				has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_navy_focus_this_year
				has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_air_focus_this_year
				has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_nuke_focus_this_year
				has_country_flag = SPR_nerd_council_gen_focus_this_year
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 15
	}
}

### Carlist Event Chains

# Carlist Succession Crisis in the Making
country_event = {
	id = sprd.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.4" }
	title = sprd.4.t
	desc = sprd.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_carlism

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.4.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.5
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# Alfonso Carlos Dies
country_event = {
	id = sprd.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.7" }
	title = sprd.7.t
	desc = sprd.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_alfonso_carlos

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SPR
		date > 1936.09.27
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = alfonso_carlos_dead
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.7.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		set_country_flag = alfonso_carlos_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.37
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}


# Javier gives another speech
country_event = {
	id = sprd.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.8" }
	title = sprd.8.t
	desc = {
		text = sprd.8.d_javier
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_carlism_chose_javier
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = sprd.8.d_carlos
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_carlism_chose_carlos
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_carlism

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.9
				days = 30
				random_days = 150
			}
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.10
				days = 30
				random_days = 150
			}
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.11
				days = 30
				random_days = 150
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.8.a #Time to ban his organisation
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_ban_carlists
		add_stability = -0.20
		set_country_flag = SPR_javier_banned
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.8.b #Arrest Javier and his followers!
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_arrest_javier
		add_stability = -0.10
		set_country_flag = SPR_javier_arrested
		hidden_effect = {
			POR = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprf.3
					days = 20
					random_days = 80
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.8.c #Praise his efforts
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_encourage_javier
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.02
		set_country_flag = SPR_javier_praised
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.8.e #Ignore the pretender
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.04
		set_country_flag = SPR_javier_ignored
	}
}

# Carlist bombing
country_event = {
	id = sprd.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.9" }
	title = sprd.9.t
	desc = sprd.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_bombing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_javier_banned
			has_country_flag = SPR_javier_arrested
			has_country_flag = SPR_javier_ignored
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = CAR
			country_exists = CNT
			has_country_flag = election_success
			has_country_flag = aftermath_of_the_civil_war
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.9
				days = 30
				random_days = 150
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.9.a
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

# Assassination of Miguel Ponte Manso de Zuniga
country_event = {
	id = sprd.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.11" }
	title = sprd.11.t
	desc = sprd.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = SPR_Miguel_Ponte_Manso_de_Zuniga_sec_ade
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_javier_banned
			has_country_flag = SPR_javier_arrested
			has_country_flag = SPR_cntfai_disband
			has_country_flag = SPR_cntfai_arrest
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = CAR
			country_exists = CNT
			has_country_flag = election_success
			has_country_flag = aftermath_of_the_civil_war
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.11.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		remove_ideas = SPR_Miguel_Ponte_Manso_de_Zuniga_sec_ade
		add_ideas = SPR_Blas_Perez_Gonzalez_sec_ade
	}
}

### CNT-FAI event chains

# AP - CNT-FAI Talks Event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.13" }
	title = sprd.13.t
	desc = sprd.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_CNT_FAI

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Options for left intro #
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.a #Demand they drop syndicalism
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1188
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.b #Demand a more moderate stance
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.07
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach2
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:radical_socialist }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_democrat }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1187
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1188
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.c #Continue the talks
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach3
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_democrat }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1187
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1188
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.e #Walk out of the meeting
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = -0.07
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach4
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1189
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	# options for center intro #
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.f #Propose a ceasefire
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach5
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1203
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.g #Demand they cut ties to france
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach6
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = totalist
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1204
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1203
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.g #Propose a coalition
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		add_stability = 0.06
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach7
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					power_balance_value  = {
						id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
						value < -0.3
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1205
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1204
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

# National CNT-FAI Protests
country_event = {
	id = sprd.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.15" }
	title = sprd.15.t
	desc = sprd.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.15.a #Send out the police!
		add_stability = -0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.15.b #Allow them to organise
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_allow_cntfai
		set_country_flag = SPR_cntfai_allowed
		clr_country_flag = SPR_cntfai_banned
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.27.a #Name him as Alfonso's successor
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SPR_future_of_the_monarchy
					option = SPR_FUTURE_OF_THE_MONARCHY_REPUBLIC
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 40
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Juan III"
			desc = "POLITICS_JUAN_BOURBON_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/SPR/Portrait_SPR_Juan_III.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = SPR_King_Juan
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.27.c #Name him as Alfonso's successor
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = 40
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jaime I"
			desc = "POLITICS_JAIME_BOURBON_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/SPR/Portrait_SPR_Jaime_I.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = SPR_King_Jaime
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}

					building = industrial_complex
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 instant_build = yes }
		}
		SPR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POR modifier = large_increase } }
		POR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SPR modifier = large_increase } }
	}
}

# Carlist Uprising begins
country_event = {
	id = sprc.1
	title = sprc.1.t
	desc = sprc.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_civwar
	timeout_days = 7
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.1"
		set_country_flag = Manuel_Fal_Conde_dead
		set_country_flag = Onesimo_Redondo_Ortega_dead
		set_country_flag = Jose_Luis_Arrese_Magra_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprc.9
				days = 3
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CAR = { exists = no } }
				CAR_setup_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sprc.1.a #We shall fight them!
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_template = "Guardias de Reserva" }
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Guardias de Reserva"
						division_names_group = SPR_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						}
						support = {
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
				}
				41 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Falange de Madrid\" division_template = \"Guardias de Reserva\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = SPR
						prioritize_location = 3938
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = sprc.5.d

	fire_only_once = no

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.5"
	}

	option = {
		name = sprc.5.a # Yes, we need those guns!
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CNT }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = 1500
				producer = FRA
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = CAR }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = 1500
				producer = ITA
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = 1500
				producer = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprc.5.b # No, let's not mortgage our future just yet
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		clr_country_flag = SCW_received_equip
		set_country_flag = { flag = SCW_received_equip days = 90 value = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = sprc.5.c # Don't talk to me about buying guns
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = SCW_no_equip_thanks
	}
}

# Main Terror check event
country_event = {
	id = sprc.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.121" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
		OR = {
			has_war_with = CAR
			has_war_with = CNT
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_of = {
					array = core_states
					var:v = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable_to_random = SPR_random
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { SPR_random > 0.92 }
				}
				country_event = sprc.122
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = sprc.121 days = 15 random_days = 20 }
	}
}

		}

			}
			add_political_power = 200
			add_stability = 0.10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_political_power > -501
				has_political_power < -100
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_political_power > -101
			}
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = spanish_postwar
			country_event = {
				id = sprc.324
				days = 90
			}
		}
	}
}

# Seizing Equatorial Guinea
country_event = {
	id = sprc.327
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.327" }
	title = sprc.327.t
	desc = sprc.327.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = MAF
			tag = GER
		}
		927 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT } #Kamerun
		297 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CNT } #Equatorial Guinea
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = sprc.327.a
		add_political_power = 20
		transfer_state = 297
		297 = {
			add_claim_by = CNT
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SPR
				}
				add_claim_by = SPR
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CAR
				}
				add_claim_by = CAR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprc.327.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}

	trigger = {}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.1191.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var < 2 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_1 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var = 2 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_2 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var = 3 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_3 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var > 3 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_4 = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
		}
	}
}

	id = sprd.2300
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.2300" }
	title = sprd.2300.t
	desc = sprd.2300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_civwar3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = MAF_Mittelafrika_Collapse
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.2300.a
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -1500
		add_war_support = 0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.2300.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_equatorial_guinea_will_be_stolen_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.2301
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}
